#####

Old Phone will be rejected during pickup if

*   * Phone is not in working condition
  * RAM/Storage/IMEI do not match or verification on Rabbit Exchange App fails
  * Screen lock or icloud lock is not disabled.
  * Phone has damages on body (bends, dents, cracks, scratches, loose panel) or screen (discoloration, dead pixels, cracks, spots, lines, traces of replacement)

#####

Exchange tip

  * If old phone is rejected during pickup, you can pay the exchange discount amount at the time of delivery by card or cash and keep the new phone
  * The “Limited-Time Discount” will not be refunded if the old item is successfully picked up

##  Mi 1year Screen Protect Plan for Smartphones Between 8000-8999 (Email
Delivery, No Physical Kit)

from Service Lee Technologies Pvt. Ltd

[ __](/product-
reviews/B0D1QWQ6T3/ref=psd_bb_r1_B0DLW427YG_B0D1QWQ6T3?ie=UTF8&showViewpoints=1)
[ (7) ](/product-
reviews/B0D1QWQ6T3/ref=psd_bb_r1_B0DLW427YG_B0D1QWQ6T3?ie=UTF8&showViewpoints=1)

  * Why Mi Screen Protect: This Mi Screen protection plan provides coverage which includes screen replacement due to any kind of accidental breakage or damage on the handset.
  * This plan Coverage begins when the Customer purchase the Plan for his Mobile Phone (“Device”) and ends on completion of one year from the date of purchase of the Plan (“Plan Term”). This warranty is applicable only on new XiaoMi product purchased at Amazon. Service charge of Rs.413/- inc. taxes is the admin fee collected by the ASC directly.
  * The screen protection plan coverage is valid up-to 2 claims during the plan period. The plan will auto-activate within 15 days of the device purchase date. No cooling period is applicable & claim will be eligible from the date of device purchase.
  * Minimal documentation is required from the customer during a claim, a one time Minimum deductible needs to be paid by the customer to XiaoMi Authorised Service Centre directly. Customers can cancel the policy maximum within 7 working days from the date of purchase.
  * How to raise a claim: Schedule a service at your convenience from your Amazon account itself by navigating to Your Orders section in your Amazon account > go to the product order > click on Get Product Support > schedule an appointment. We use genuine spare parts & repairs carried out through Mi Authorized service centres.

##  10 days Service Centre Replacement

Replacement Reason  |  Replacement Period  |  Replacement Policy   
---|---|---  
Physical Damage,  
Wrong and Missing Item  |  10 days from delivery  |  Replacement   
Defective Item  |  10 days from delivery  |  Redmi warranty policy (at Service Centre)   
  
__

Defective item:

  * Amazon may provide support via self-help guides or on call or at doorstep, as applicable. 
  * If this issue is not resolved, please contact Redmi or visit the Service Centre.
  * Redmi will repair the product or provide a replacement or Defective certificate, as applicable. The time taken for resolution will be as per Redmi warranty policies.
  * Please check for nearest Brand service center in your location. For details [ click here ](https://www.amazon.in/gp/help/customer/display.html?ie=UTF8&nodeId=202064020)

  
Physical Damage, Wrong, Missing Items:

  * Returns will not be accepted if it is an Open Box Delivery order
  * Remote verification by image/video will be done by Amazon

  *   * 

  * ### 

Does the Redmi A4 5G support 5G network?

Yes, the Redmi A4 5G supports SA networks and works with telecom operators
that provide SA 5G connectivity. Please check availability of Standalone 5G
with your networks provider.

  * ### 

Does the Redmi A4 5G support dual 5G SIM connectivity?

No, the Redmi A4 5G does not support dual 5G SIM connectivity. It allows 5G on
one SIM card, while the second SIM slot is limited to 4G connectivity.

  * ### 

What is SA and NSA?

SA stands for Standalone. SA networks use a dedicated 5G core network, which
allows them to fully leverage 5G's capabilities. NSA stands for Non-Standalone
and uses the existing 4G network.

  * ### 

What kind of display does Redmi A4 5G have?

The Redmi A4 5G features a large 17.47 cm (6.88") HD+ display with 600 nits
brightness and an adjustable 120Hz refresh rate for smooth scrolling

  * ### 

Does the Redmi A4 5G support fast charging, and what is its battery capacity?

The Redmi A4 5G is equipped with a 5160mAh battery, providing reliable all-day
battery life. It supports 18W fast charging and comes with a 33W in-box
charge, valued at ₹1999, ensuring quick and convenient charging right out of
the box.

[__How are ratings calculated?](javascript:void\(0\))

To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we
don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how
recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also
analyses reviews to verify trustworthiness.

Sponsored ****

### Customers say

Customers find the phone good value for money and appreciate its design,
particularly the amazing display and glass back. The phone's performance
receives mixed feedback - while some praise its speed, others report it being
dead slow. Functionality is also mixed, with some saying it works well while
others report issues with 5G not working. Battery life and display quality get
mixed reviews, with some praising the battery backup while others complain
about quick drainage, and while some like the screen size, others find the
image quality poor. The phone hanging issue is a significant concern, with
multiple customers reporting this problem.

##### [ _5.0 out of 5 stars_ 📱 Redmi A4 5G – Budget-Friendly Beast!
](/gp/customer-reviews/R2JJ25I8JQA69Q/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)

Reviewed in India on 25 July 2025

Colour: Sparkle Purple __Size: 4GB+64GB __Verified Purchase

After using the Redmi A4 5G, I’m genuinely impressed by its overall
performance. The quality of this device is solid, especially for the price it
comes at. Whether you're browsing, streaming, or gaming, it delivers a smooth
experience without any lags. And the battery backup? Fantastic. It easily
powers through a full day—even with heavy usage.  
  
The phone feels well-built and reliable, making it a smart choice for anyone
looking for affordability without compromising on capability. It’s one of
those rare finds where performance, design, and battery life come together
perfectly.  
  
If you’re in the market for a dependable 5G phone that doesn’t break the bank,
this one should definitely be on your radar. 👍

##### [ _4.0 out of 5 stars_ Best Budget 5G Smartphone for Students – Great
Value! ](/gp/customer-reviews/R7DR1QJL9RRQG/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)

Reviewed in India on 20 July 2025

Colour: Sparkle Purple __Size: 4GB+128GB __Verified Purchase

I unboxed the Redmi A4 5G today, and I’m genuinely impressed with the first-
day experience.  
The phone looks stylish and feels light in hand.  
✅ The display is bright and large, making it perfect for reading PDFs and
watching YouTube videos.  
✅ Performance is smooth thanks to the Snapdragon 4 Gen 2 processor – great for
apps like WhatsApp, Chrome, YouTube, and basic study needs.  
✅ The 5G network connected instantly (tested with Jio SIM) and offers
excellent speed.  
✅ The battery easily lasts a full day with moderate usage like browsing,
calls, and video lectures.  
✅ You get 128GB storage, which is perfect for storing documents, videos, and
photos.  
  
\---  
  
👍 What I liked:  
  
Excellent 5G support in this price range  
  
Clean and smooth HyperOS experience  
  
Lightweight and premium-looking design  
  
Ideal for students and budget users  
  
\---  
  
👎 What could be better:  
  
Camera is average, especially in low light  
  
18W charging is a bit slow (takes about 2 hours to full charge)  
  
\---  
  
🎯 Final Verdict:  
  
If you’re a student or looking for a reliable 5G phone under ₹10,000 with
decent performance and good storage, Redmi A4 5G is a solid option. Totally
worth it for daily use, online classes, and light multitasking.  
  
\---  
  
✍️ Reviewer Name:  
  
Rajendra Singh Bhati
